//===================================================================================================================
												//-------------------- Class #27 || Laravel Queue (applied in mail) --------------------
//===================================================================================================================
			-- Laravel Queues doc link: https://laravel.com/docs/8.x/queues
			-- Laravel Task Schedule doc link: https://laravel.com/docs/8.x/scheduling
			
			-- amra jokhon amader ei project e Email patai tkn dekte pari j amader ei mail ta jethe ektu time nei, mane browser mail ta patanor somoy beshi somoy dhore reload nei, because amra jokon mail patacchi tkn ta SMTP te request patacche, erpor jokon shee response pacche tkn shee frontend theke mane user er data gula send korteche, that means server to server communication hocche, ei same kaj jodi oneke kore mane website e 1000+ eksathe message/mail patathe pare, taile tkn kinto problem hobe, because eksathe shee 1000+ connection make korbe, So er solution hisebe laravel e ei dhororner kaj gula background e rekhe deya jai, & aste aste ekta ekta kore dispatch hothe thakbe, dispatch howa mane jokon suppose 1000+ request job asbe tkn shee eksathe ei sob korbe na, shee ekta job list make korbe then ekta dhorbe, oita shesh hole arekta dhorbe, eivabe korar fole may be kaj ta korte 5minute time beshi lagbe, but server e kono pressure porbe na, So eta ekta life saving/server saving matter, ei jinister jonno laravel e "laravel Queue schedule" name e documentation e dekte pabo, link: ( https://laravel.com/docs/8.x/queues ).
			
			-- ekn amra direct kaj e chole jacchi: 
					-- 1 -- apply_command: php artisan queue:table
										-- eta dile queue er jonno amader magration table(jobs name e) make hobe. ei name e: 2022_01_31_073236_create_jobs_table.php
										-- link: https://laravel.com/docs/8.x/queues#database
										
					-- 2 -- command: php artisan migrate
					
					-- 3 -- in .env file ---------- QUEUE_CONNECTION=database
					
					-- 4 -- apply_command: php artisan make:job ProcessEnquireEmail
										-- eta dile queue er jonno amader magration table(jobs name e) make hobe.
										-- link: https://laravel.com/docs/8.x/queues#creating-jobs
					
					-- 5 -- in .env file ---------- QUEUE_CONNECTION=database
					
					-- 6 -- command: php artisan make:job ProcessEnquireEmail
					
					-- 7 -- in controller:-- ProcessEnquireEmail::dispatch($data);
					
					-- 8 -- in ProcessEnquireEmail.php:-- Mail::send(new EnquireEmail($this->enquireData)); //++ opore variable(enquireData) niye data rakar kaj ta korte hobe,
			
			
		//--------------------------------------------- 2022_01_31_073236_create_jobs_table.php ---------------------------------------------------------------------
					-- apply_command: php artisan queue:table
					-- kono kicho change korte hobe na, default ja chilo tai rekhe migrate kore dibo.
					-- command: php artisan migrate
					
						Schema::create('jobs', function (Blueprint $table) {
							$table->bigIncrements('id');
							$table->string('queue')->index();
							$table->longText('payload');
							$table->unsignedTinyInteger('attempts');
							$table->unsignedInteger('reserved_at')->nullable();
							$table->unsignedInteger('available_at');
							$table->unsignedInteger('created_at');
						});

		//---------------------------------------------------------- .env ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
						// QUEUE_CONNECTION=sync 		//eta default chilo, otar bodole nicher ta dibo
						QUEUE_CONNECTION=database
						
						
		-- command: php artisan make:job ProcessEnquireEmail
				-- ei command deyar sathe sathe amder ekta file create hobe "ProcessEnquireEmail.php" name e, jar directory holo: "app/Jobs/ProcessEnquireEmail.php"
		
		-- in controller:-- ProcessEnquireEmail::dispatch($data);
		-- in ProcessEnquireEmail.php:-- Mail::send(new EnquireEmail($this->enquireData)); //++ opore variable(enquireData) niye data rakar kaj ta korte hobe,
		
		-- Now ekn amader k dispatch korte hobe job ta controller e, documentation_link: https://laravel.com/docs/8.x/queues#dispatching-jobs
		-- amra jokon kono ekta mail patabo userEnd theke tkn ta sathe satehi dekahbe mail send, time/reload e beshi somoy nibe na, & ta database e queue e job ta save hobe, but tkn kinto mail ta send hoye jai ni, amader k ei job ta chalalor/howar jonno amader ei queue ta k run korte hobe, amara localhost e eta manually command(php artisan queue:work or php artisan queue:list) diye run kori, && server/live_server e amra eita k corn_job chaliye run kore dei always
		
		-- command: php artisan queue:list
		-- command: php artisan queue:work
		
						
		//--------------------------------------------- app/Http/Controllers/PropertyController.php ---------------------------------------------------------------------
					public function enquire(Request $request, $propertyID)
						{
							$request->validate([
								'name'  => ['required', 'max:255'],
								'phone' => ['required', 'max:255'],
								'email' => ['email', 'required', 'max:255'],
								'message' => ['required', 'max:255']
							]);

							// $request->message .= '\nThis message was sent from '. route('property.show',$propertyID) . ' website.';

							PropertyEnquire::create([
								'name'  => $request->name,
								'phone'  => $request->phone,
								'email'  => $request->email,
								'message'  => $request->message . '\nThis message was sent from '. route('property.show',$propertyID) . ' website.',
							]);

							// Send User & Admin mail/message
							$data = [$request->all(), 'propertyURL' => route('property.show', $propertyID)];

							// Send User & Admin mail/message via Queue
							ProcessEnquireEmail::dispatch($data);								//-------------------------------------------------------------------
							// Mail::send(new EnquireEmail($data));     // Send User & Admin mail/message via normal way

							return redirect()->back()->with(['message'=>'Message sent successfully']);
						}
						
						
		//--------------------------------------------- app/Jobs/ProcessEnquireEmail.php ---------------------------------------------------------------------
						<?php

						namespace App\Jobs;

						use App\Mail\EnquireEmail;
						use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Mail;
						use Illuminate\Bus\Queueable;
						use Illuminate\Contracts\Queue\ShouldBeUnique;
						use Illuminate\Contracts\Queue\ShouldQueue;
						use Illuminate\Foundation\Bus\Dispatchable;
						use Illuminate\Queue\InteractsWithQueue;
						use Illuminate\Queue\SerializesModels;

						class ProcessEnquireEmail implements ShouldQueue
						{
							use Dispatchable, InteractsWithQueue, Queueable, SerializesModels;


							public $enquireData;									//----------------------------------------

							/**
							 * Create a new job instance.
							 *
							 * @return void
							 */
							public function __construct($data)										//----------------------------------------
							{
								$this->enquireData = $data;										//----------------------------------------
							}

							/**
							 * Execute the job.
							 *
							 * @return void
							 */
							public function handle()
							{
								Mail::send(new EnquireEmail($this->enquireData));										//----------------------------------------
							}
						}
						
						
		//-------------------------------------------------------- app/Mail/EnquireEmail.php ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
						<?php

							namespace App\Mail;

							use Illuminate\Bus\Queueable;
							use Illuminate\Contracts\Queue\ShouldQueue;
							use Illuminate\Mail\Mailable;
							use Illuminate\Queue\SerializesModels;

							class EnquireEmail extends Mailable
							{
								use Queueable, SerializesModels;


								public $enquireData;

								public function __construct($data)
								{
									$this->enquireData = $data;
								}

								/**
								 * Build the message.
								 *
								 * @return $this
								 */
								public function build()
								{
									return $this->view('emails.enquire-email')->to($this->enquireData[0]['email'])->from('propertylisting@civanolo.com')->subject('Property Enquire')->with('data',$this->enquireData);
								}
							}

						
		//-- evabe amra "queues" diye onek rokomer kaj korte parbo, ekhane just mail ta dekhano hoyeche summary vabe, ProcessEnquireEmail.php file er handle() method er moddhe amra amader jabotiyo proyojonio sob php code likte parbo, for example: ekahane amara jodi chai amader property create er beparta amra ei queues diye korbo, taile amra ei "ProcessEnquireEmail.php" file er handle() method e eshe property_create er code gual likte parbo.

//============================================================================================================
												//-------------------- Class #28 || Currency Change --------------------
//============================================================================================================

		-- amra ekhane currency change dekbo, mane amader ekahne website e 2ta currency system ache ekta Doller arekta Taka, nav bar e ei currency gula sign button akare deya ache, amra ei currency button gula te click kore currency gula change korbo, R egula amra change korbo User er browser er "cookie" te rekhe, mane amara ekahne COOKIE use korbo, Cookie amra amader browser k inspect korle "Application" er moddhe cookie dekte pabo,
		
		-- Cookie::queue('currency', $code, 3600);		//--ekhane queue er parameters e 3ta perameter royeche ekahen, 1st er holo amra cookie te amra eta ki 'name' e save korbo, R 2nd parameter holo route theke 'code' ta asbe, R 3rd parameter holo ei cookie ta kotho minute stay korbe(ekhane 3600 minute stay korbe).
		
		-- Currency Converter API : $get = Http::get('https://freecurrencyapi.net/api/v2/latest?apikey=76c89170-6178-11ec-98f1-5f7ce0abde0a&base_currency=TRY');
		
		
		//--------------------------------------------- resources/views/components/header.blade.php ----------------------------------------------------------------
					<a class="inline-block text-xl rounded-full px-3 py-1 text-white" href="{{ route('currency', 'usd') }}" title="Change Currency to Doller">$</a>
					<a class="inline-block text-xl rounded-full px-3 py-1 text-white" href="{{ route('currency', 'tl') }}" title="Change Currency to Lira">₺</a>
					<a class="inline-block text-2xl rounded-full px-3 py-1 text-white" href="{{ route('currency', 'bdt') }}" title="Change Currency to Taka">৳</a>
		
		//--------------------------------------------- routes/web.php -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
						Route::group(['prefix' => LaravelLocalization::setLocale()], function () {
								// Currency Change
								Route::get('/currency-change/{code}', [HomeController::class, 'currencyConverter'])->name('currency');
						});
						
		//--------------------------------------------- app/Http/Controllers/HomeController.php -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
						use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Cookie;
						
						public function currencyConverter($code)
						{
							Cookie::queue('currency', $code, 3600);
							return back();
							
							//queue er parameters e 3ta perameter royeche ekahen, 1st er holo amra cookie te amra eta ki 'name' e save korbo, R 2nd parameter holo route theke 'code' ta asbe, R 3rd parameter holo ei cookie ta kotho minute stay korbe(ekhane 3600 minute stay korbe).
						}
		
		//--------------------------------------------- app/Models/Property.php --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
						<?php

							namespace App\Models;

							use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Factories\HasFactory;
							use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
							use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Cookie;									//---------------------------------
							use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Http;									//---------------------------------

							class Property extends Model
							{
								use HasFactory;

								protected $fillable = [
									'name','name_tr','featured_image','location_id','price','sale','type','bedrooms','drawing_rooms','bathrooms','net_sqm','gross_sqm','pool','overview','overview_tr','why_buy','why_buy_tr','description','description_tr',
								];
								// protected $guarded = ['created_at', 'updated_at'];
								// protected $hidden = ['created_at', 'updated_at'];


								//    public function featured() {
								//        $this->belongsTo(Media::class, 'featured_media_id');
								//    }

								public function location() {
									return $this->belongsTo(Location::class, 'location_id');
								}

								public function gallery() {
									return $this->hasMany(Media::class, 'property_id');
								}

								public function dynamic_pricing($lira) {					//----------------------------------------
									$current_currency = Cookie::get('currency', 'tl');  //ekhane Cookie::get('key':'currency', default:'tl'); mane default lira(tl) raktechi amra currency website e.
									if($current_currency == 'usd') {
										$get = Http::get('https://freecurrencyapi.net/api/v2/latest?apikey=76c89170-6178-11ec-98f1-5f7ce0abde0a&base_currency=TRY');
										if($get->successful()) {
											$usd = intval($lira * $get->json()['data']['USD']);
											$usd = number_format($usd, 2);
											return $usd . ' USD';
										}
									}
									elseif($current_currency == 'bdt'){
										$get = Http::get('https://freecurrencyapi.net/api/v2/latest?apikey=76c89170-6178-11ec-98f1-5f7ce0abde0a&base_currency=TRY');
										if($get->successful()) {
											$bdt = intval($lira * $get->json()['data']['BDT']);
											$bdt = number_format($bdt, 2);
											return $bdt . ' BDT';
										}
									} else {
										$lira = number_format($lira, 2);
										return $lira . ' TL';
									}
								}

							}

		//--------------------------------------------- resources/views/components/single-property-card.blade.php -------------------------------------------------------------
							<h3 class="text-2xl py-3">{{ $property->dynamic_pricing($property->price) }}</h3>
							
		//--------------------------------------------- resources/views/property/single.blade.php -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
						<h3 class="text-lg mt-2">{{ __('Price') }}: <span class="text-red-800">
									{{-- {{ number_format($property->price, 2, ',', ',') }} TK</span> --}}
									{{-- {{ number_format($property->price) }} {{ __('Tk') }}</span> --}}
									{{ $property->dynamic_pricing($property->price) }}
						</h3>

//------------------//---------------------//---------------------//------------------------//-------------------------//-------------------------//------------------------//--------------------







//=========================================================================================================================
												//-------------------- Class #29 || Cloudways deployment --------------------
//=========================================================================================================================
			-- YouTube Rasel_vai: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=kE7HK8nY1x4&list=PLhPBqF--77ImGEZE6xSS62UVegQOIgP4g&index=30
			-- YouTube: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=VpIyUGsvPNU
			-- Doc blog: https://www.cloudways.com/en/
			-- Doc blog: https://platform.cloudways.com/server/create
			-- Doc blog: https://trendslearner.com/how-to-verify-a-new-cloudways-account-simple-verification-process/
			
			-- At first "Cloudways" e account kore login korle amra( https://platform.cloudways.com/server ) navbar e kicho option/menu dekte pabo, segula holo: 'Servers', 'Applications' etc, ekn 1st e amader k "Servers" e giye ekta server launch/create korte hobe, then "Applications" e eshe ekta project create kore nibo, erpor amader make kora oi "Applications" e 'project' tai click korbo, onno ekta details page e niye jabe, jekhane amader k Database er DBname, username, password etc show korbo onnanno details info shoho, ekn amra GitHub er sathe eta k connect korbo, tai left-side er menu-bar theke "Deployment Via Git" option e click korbo, tkn oi page e amader k ekta SSH key generate korte bolbe ja oikahne thaka "Generate SSH Key" button e click kore "View SSH Key" button e click korlei show hobe, amra ota(SSH key ta) copy kore nibo. erpor amra GitHub er project-repository(property-listing) te jabo amader, then horizontal nav-bar theke jabo "Settings" then jabo left-bar theke "Deploy Keys" option e, then "Add Deploy Key" button e click kore title(cloudways) + copy kora SSH key ta input box e diye & niche "allow write access" checkbox tai uncheck obostai rekhe save korbo. erpor amra abar amader project-repository(property-listing) e jabo okhane "code" button(jekha tkeke amra repository ta clone korar link copy kori) theke "SSH" option theke link ta copy korbo, then now amra abar amader "Cloudways" er oi "Deployment Via Git" er "View SSH Key" generate korechilam oi page e giye "Git Remote Address" option e amader github-project-repository theke copy kore ana SSH link ta bosiye "authenticate" button e click korbo. then "Start Deployment" button e click korbo. 
			-- ekn amader k ei server e SSH diye login korte hobe, ei jonno amra ekn amader project directory er pc er command_prompt/terminal e jabo, 
					-- er aghe amader k ei server er project er Credential mane Username, Password gula lagbe, egula amra left-bar er 1st menu ta "Master Credential" OR  Application_Management er "Access Details" option er "Application Credential" e pabo, okhan credential gula make kora na thakle amra add new kore username+password make kore nibo.
					-- then laft-bar er nicher dikhe "Application Settings" option e giye "SSH Access" enable kore dibo.
								-- doc_link: https://support.cloudways.com/en/articles/5121251-how-to-enable-ssh-access-for-application-users
					-- ekn amader project directory er  pc er command_prompt/terminal e jabo okhane giye comman dibo:
								-- command: ssh suzan@178.62.95.226		//command tar syntex holo: sss username@public_ip 	//ei creadintial gula "Application Credential" theke paowa creadintial gula
								-- erpor password chaibe, password dibo	(Suzancse#16)	//password will not become visible due to security reasons.
											-- doc_link: https://support.cloudways.com/en/articles/5119485-guide-to-connecting-to-your-application-using-ssh-sftp
								-- ekn command: ls 	//dile amara amader laravel er project file gula dekte pabo, mane amra ekn project directory tei achi, tai amra ekn ekhane laravel install kore pelte parbo.
								-- ekn laravel install er aghe amader k .env make korte hobe, env amra 2vabe korte pari, SFTP login kore korte pari OR terminal theke pari, 
											--  pc er command_prompt/terminal e: nano .env
														-- ei command deyar fole amader terminal e amader .env file ta show hobe okhane amra amader server(cloudways) theke (Applications/Access Details) Database er Name, Username, Password sob niye copy kore .env file e bosai dibo. ekhane jodio amra env te opore project url, project name egulao bosiye diyechi.
														-- then exit er jonno command dibo: CTRL+x
														-- then yes er jonno y
														-- then enter button
											-- erpor abar terminal/command_prompt/terminal e dibo: composer install
											-- erpor abar terminal/command_prompt/terminal e dibo: php artisan optimize:clear	//jeto env change korechi, route cache jeno clear hoye jai.
											-- erpor abar terminal/command_prompt/terminal e dibo: php artisan migrate:fresh --seed
			-- ekn amra amader oi "Application URL"( http://phplaravel-724963-2416001.cloudwaysapps.com/ ) e gele amader project ta live dekte parbo,
			
			-- ekn jodi amra laravel project tai github repository te kono kicho code edit/change kore push kori & ta amader ie live server e dekte hole amader ei cloudways server e pull kore nicthe hobe, er jonno "Applications" er left-bar theke "Deployment Via Git" option e giye "Pull" button click kore pull kore nicthe hobe,

//=====================================================================================================================
												//------------- Class #30 - Cloudways github action automatic --------------//
//=====================================================================================================================

			-- YouTube Resel_vai: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=xeHbptzpXSE&list=PLhPBqF--77ImGEZE6xSS62UVegQOIgP4g&index=30
			-- Website: https://github.com/features/actions
			
			-- ekhane amra cloudways er sathe github action kivabe automated korbo ta dekbo, amra jodi ekn github er nav er "marketplace" ( https://github.com/marketplace ) e giye okhane search bar e 'cloudways' likhe search dei taile "Cloudways API Git Pull" ( https://github.com/marketplace/actions/cloudways-api-git-pull ) eita pabo,
			
			-- Nicher kaj gula ei ektu aghe paowa "cloudways-api-git-pull" page e ache( link: https://github.com/marketplace/actions/cloudways-api-git-pull ), ekn amra amader project e giye root e ".github" name e ekta folder create korbo github er jonno, then er moddhe "workflows" name e ekta folder create kore er moddhe "cloudways-deploy.yml" name e ekta file create korbo, mane flow/directory ta holo: ( .github/workflows/cloudways-deploy.yml )
			-- ekn ei "cloudways-deploy.yml" file er vitore amader code likte hobe documentation theke
			-- ekn amra github e "secrets" add korbo, eita ektu privacy royeche, onnora pele problem, ei 'secrets'  add korte gele amader "github-project-repo-->top-nav theke "settings"-->left-nav theke "secrets/actions secret" e jabo, then "new repository secret" button e click kore "Name" field e "CLOUDWAYS_EMAIL" dibo, & "Value" field e "amar oi cloudways er email ta dibo" then add korbo, evabe baki secrets gulao add kore nithe hobe,
			-- ekn project er ".github/workflows/cloudways-deploy.yml" e giye nicher code likhe dibo
						//--------------------------------- .github/workflows/cloudways-deploy.yml ---------------------------------------------
									name: Cloudways API Git Pull

									on: push

									jobs:
									  tag:
										name: New Tag

										runs-on: ubuntu-latest

										steps:
										  - name: Checkout Code
											uses: actions/checkout@v2

										  - name: Cloudways API Git Pull
											uses: roelmagdaleno/cloudways-api-git-pull-action@stable
											with:
											  email: ${{ secrets.CLOUDWAYS_EMAIL }}
											  api-key: ${{ secrets.CLOUDWAYS_API_KEY }}
											  server-id: ${{ secrets.CLOUDWAYS_SERVER_ID }}
											  app-id: ${{ secrets.CLOUDWAYS_APP_ID }}
											  branch-name: ${{ secrets.CLOUDWAYS_BRANCH_NAME }}
											  deploy-path: ''
											  
			-- ekn kicho change kore push korle ta direct automatic push hobe server e.

													//----------- Class #31 || feather Icons || Lity lightbox --------------//
//=======================================================================================================================

			//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
													//-------- feather Icons -------// 
			//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
				-- amra Icon er jonno ei "feather icon" use korte pari, eta font-awesome er motho or font-awesome er alternative,
				-- link: https://feathericons.com/
				-- link: https://github.com/feathericons/feather#feather
				-- YouTube Rasel_vai: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ubiKiesns4E&list=PLhPBqF--77ImGEZE6xSS62UVegQOIgP4g&index=31
				
				//---------- Usages: -------------------------------
						-- 1 -- npm install feather-icons --save
						-- 2 -- project/resources/js/app.js
											require('./bootstrap');
											import feather from 'feather-icons/dist/feather.min'
											feather.replace();
						-- 3 -- in blade file: <i data-feather="circle"></i>
						-- 4 -- in resources/css/app.css file: 
											.feather {
												@apply inline-block
											}
						-- 5 -- npm run watch


			//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
													//-------- Lity lightbox -------// 
			//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
						-- image/play youtube video te click korle Boro kore pop-up er moto open hoye play/open hobe erkom er kaje amra eta use korte pari.(example hisebe), its a lightbox.
						-- link: https://sorgalla.com/lity/
						-- link: https://www.npmjs.com/package/lity
						
						//---------- Usages: -------------------------------
								-- 1 -- lity er file download korte hobe, ekhane oi file er moddhe dist folder er moddhe 3ta file thakbe(lity.css, lity.js, jquery.js)
								-- 2 -- ekn amader jquery.js aghe theke project e install chilo(resources/js/app.js e), tai eta new vabe link kore nai, baki lity.css+lity.js file 2ta link korate hobe, ekn lity.css file ta ene amader project er "resources/css" folder e rekhe "resources/css/app.css" e link mane import(@import 'lity.min.css';) kore dithe pari, or ei "lity.css" file er code gula direct ei "resources/css/app.css" e paste kore dithe pari taile ar abar extra vabe link/import kora laglo na,........... ekn lity.js file ta ene amader project er "resources/js" folder e rekhe "resources/css/app.js" e link mane require (require('./lity.min');) kore dithe pari,
								-- 3 -- project/resources/js/app.css -----------
												-- ekn lity.css file ta ene amader project er "resources/css" folder e rekhe "resources/css/app.css" e link mane import(@import 'lity.min.css';) kore dithe pari, or ei "lity.css" file er code gula direct ei "resources/css/app.css" e paste kore dithe pari taile ar abar extra vabe link/import kora laglo na,
														-- @import 'lity.min.css';
								-- 4 -- in resources/css/app.js file --------------
												-- ekn lity.js file ta ene amader project er "resources/js" folder e rekhe "resources/css/app.js" e link mane require (require('./lity.min');) kore dithe pari,
								-- 5 -- npm run watch
								-- 6 -- in blade file: ------------
													<a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=XSGBVzeBUbk" data-lity>iFrame Youtube</a>
								-- 6 -- baki useage gula documentation e bola ache.
